34 /**
35   * inserts the CIResponsibleParty into the MDMetadata XML (where needed)
36   *
37   * @param xml
38   */
39 private class AddCIResponsiblePartyToMDMetadata(xml: Node) extends RewriteRule {
40   override def transform(n: Node): Seq[Node] = n match {
41     case e: Elem if (e.label == "contact" && e.prefix == "gmd")
42       || (e.label == "pointOfContact" && e.prefix == "gmd") => {
43       new Elem(e.prefix, e.label, e.attributes, e.scope, e.minimizeEmpty, (xml).toSeq: _*)
44     }
45     case x => x
46   }
47 }
48 
49 /**
50   * inserts the distributionInfo into the MDMetadata XML (where needed)
51   *
52   * @param xml
53   */
54 private class AddMDDistributionToMDMetadata(xml: Node) extends RewriteRule {
55   override def transform(n: Node): Seq[Node] = n match {
56     case e: Elem if (e.label == "distributionInfo" && e.prefix == "gmd") => {
57       new Elem(e.prefix, e.label, e.attributes, e.scope, e.minimizeEmpty, (xml).toSeq: _*)
58     }
59     case x => x
60   }
61 }
62 
63 trait Xmlable {
64   /**
65     * creates JsValue from this class
66     *
67     * @return JsValue
68     */
69   def toXml(): Node
70 }
71 
72 trait Jsonable {
73   /**
74     * creates JsValue from this class
75     *
76     * @return JsValue
77     */
78   def toJson(): JsValue
79 }
80 
81 trait JsonableCompanion[A] extends ClassnameLogger {
82   val reads: Reads[A]
83   val writes: Writes[A]
84   val format: Format[A] = Format(reads, writes)
85 
86   /**
87     * parseOm2Measurements object from Json
88     *
89     * @param json
90     * @return Option if parsing error
91     */
92   def fromJson(json: JsValue): Option[A]
93 }

268 object MdMetadata extends ClassnameLogger with JsonableCompanion[MdMetadata] {
269 
270   override implicit val reads: Reads[MdMetadata] = (
271     (JsPath \ "fileIdentifier").read[String](Reads.filterNot[String](ValidationError("String empty"))(_.trim().isEmpty))
272       or Reads.pure(UUID.randomUUID().toString)
273       and
274       (JsPath \ "title").read[String] and
275       (JsPath \ "abstrakt").read[String] and
276       (JsPath \ "keywords").read[List[String]] and
277       (JsPath \ "smartCategory").read[List[String]] and
278       (JsPath \ "topicCategoryCode").read[String] and
279       (JsPath \ "hierarchyLevelName").read[String] and
280       (JsPath \ "scale").read[String] and
281       (JsPath \ "extent").read[MdMetadataExtent] and
282       (JsPath \ "citation").read[MdMetadataCitation] and
283       (JsPath \ "lineageStatement").read[String] and
284       (JsPath \ "responsibleParty").read[MdMetadataResponsibleParty] and
285       (JsPath \ "distribution").read[MdMetadataDistribution]
286     ) (MdMetadata.apply _)
287 
288   override implicit val writes: Writes[MdMetadata] = (
289     (JsPath \ "fileIdentifier").write[String] and
290       (JsPath \ "title").write[String] and
291       (JsPath \ "abstrakt").write[String] and
292       (JsPath \ "keywords").write[List[String]] and
293       (JsPath \ "smartCategory").write[List[String]] and
294       (JsPath \ "topicCategoryCode").write[String] and
295       (JsPath \ "hierarchyLevelName").write[String] and
296       (JsPath \ "scale").write[String] and
297       (JsPath \ "extent").write[MdMetadataExtent] and
298       (JsPath \ "citation").write[MdMetadataCitation] and
299       (JsPath \ "lineageStatement").write[String] and
300       (JsPath \ "responsibleParty").write[MdMetadataResponsibleParty] and
301       (JsPath \ "distribution").write[MdMetadataDistribution]
302     ) (unlift(MdMetadata.unapply))
303 
304   def fromJson(json: JsValue): Option[MdMetadata] = {
305     Json.fromJson[MdMetadata](json) match {
306       case JsSuccess(r: MdMetadata, path: JsPath) => Some(r)
307       case e: JsError => {
308         val lines = e.errors.map { tupleAction =>
309           val jsPath = tupleAction._1
310           val valErrors = tupleAction._2.map(valErr => valErr.message).toList.mkString(" ; ")
311           jsPath.toJsonString + " >> " + valErrors
312         }
313 
314         logger.error(s"JsError info  ${lines.mkString(" | ")}")
315         None
316       }
317     }
318   }
